two slashes means we may have authority but definitely means we're either matching net_path or abs_path. these two productions are ambiguous in that every net_path (except those containing an ipv6reference) is an abs_path. rfc 2396 resolves this ambiguity by applying a greedy left most matching rule. try matching net_path first and if that fails we don't have authority so then attempt to match abs_path. net_path = "" authority [ abs_path ] abs_path = "/" path_segments	WITHOUT_CLASSIFICATION	0.99598792150101	WITHOUT_CLASSIFICATION	0.004012078498990014	DESIGN
